<div id="primary" class="content-area">
	<div class="content-container site-container">
		<div id="main" class="site-main">
			<div class="woocommerce kadence-woo-messages-none-woo-pages woocommerce-notices-wrapper"></div>			<div class="content-wrap">
				<article id="post-10205" class="entry content-bg single-entry post-10205 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-desserts">
	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		
<div class="entry-content single-content">
	
<p>Healthier Vegan and Gluten Free Apple Pie Cups are what you need even though it&#8217;s not quite fall! cozy season or not, if you love apples, these are everything you could want in a healthy dessert and more.</p>



<p>the crust is AMAZING, like i have to say, it&#8217;s 10/10. the fact that the crust is gluten free just makes Healthier Vegan and Gluten Free Apple Pie Cups even better. </p>



<p>putting Healthier Vegan and Gluten Free Apple Pie Cups is a totally seamless process!</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" src="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/1-6.jpeg" alt="" class="wp-image-10206" width="892" height="1189" srcset="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/1-6.jpeg 600w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/1-6-225x300.jpeg 225w" sizes="(max-width: 892px) 100vw, 892px" /></figure>
</div>


<p>the crust is made in a food processor and then the apples are sautéed in a pan.</p>



<p>when it comes to the crust, that bakes twice. once by itself and once with the apple filling inside.</p>



<p>you need two medium-large honey crisp apples for the filling, but you can use whatever variety that you can get ahold of.</p>



<p>honey crisp are my favorite and i highly recommend them for the best flavor possible.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" src="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/2-7.jpeg" alt="" class="wp-image-10207" width="892" height="1086" srcset="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/2-7.jpeg 657w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/2-7-246x300.jpeg 246w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/2-7-600x731.jpeg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 892px) 100vw, 892px" /></figure>
</div>


<p>just a heads up, the dough for the crust is a bit sticky, and this is totally normal. you should add the dough to parchment lined cups and then slightly wet your fingers.</p>



<p>after that, lightly press on the dough edges and form a wide hole in the center. </p>



<p>the crusts then bake in the oven for 20 minutes. after you pull them out, quickly, gently and safely use a tbsp measuring spoon to press down the center because it will rise in the baking process.</p>



<p>you can serve Healthier Vegan and Gluten Free Apple Pie Cups with vegan vanilla ice cream, yogurt or coconut cream.</p>



<p>it&#8217;s a little too soon, but Healthier Vegan and Gluten Free Apple Pie Cups would make excellent desserts during the holiday season. </p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" src="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/3-5.jpeg" alt="" class="wp-image-10208" width="893" height="1123" srcset="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/3-5.jpeg 636w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/3-5-239x300.jpeg 239w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/3-5-600x755.jpeg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 893px) 100vw, 893px" /></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>here&#8217;s everything you need to make Healthier Vegan and Gluten Free Apple Pie Cups</strong></p>



<p>oat flour</p>



<p>almond flour</p>



<p>tapioca flour</p>



<p>baking powder</p>



<p>runny almond butter</p>



<p>maple syrup</p>



<p>dairy free milk</p>



<p>vanilla extract</p>



<p>cinnamon</p>



<p>honey crisp apples</p>



<p>coconut oil</p>



<p>coconut cream</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large is-resized"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" src="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Pinterest-template-blue-337-683x1024.png" alt="" class="wp-image-10209" width="894" height="1340" srcset="https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Pinterest-template-blue-337-683x1024.png 683w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Pinterest-template-blue-337-200x300.png 200w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Pinterest-template-blue-337-768x1152.png 768w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Pinterest-template-blue-337-750x1125.png 750w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Pinterest-template-blue-337-600x900.png 600w, https://upbeetandkaleingitblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/Pinterest-template-blue-337.png 1000w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 894px) 100vw, 894px" /></figure>
</div>

      <h2 class="wprm-recipe-name wprm-block-text-bold">Healthier Vegan and Gluten Free Apple Pie Cups</h2>

    <div class="wprm-layout-column wprm-column-width-50 meadow-main-right">
      <div id="recipe-23093-instructions" class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container wprm-recipe-23093-instructions-container wprm-block-text-normal" data-recipe="23093"><h3 class="wprm-recipe-header wprm-recipe-instructions-header wprm-block-text-bold wprm-align-left wprm-header-decoration-spacer wprm-header-has-actions" style="">Method<div class="wprm-decoration-spacer"></div>&nbsp;</h3><div class="wprm-spacer" style="height: 15px;"></div><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group"><ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions"><li id="wprm-recipe-23093-step-0-0" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">preheat the oven to 350 degrees.</div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-23093-step-0-1" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">mix the crust ingredients in a food processor until a thick dough forms. it will be on the sticky side.</div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-23093-step-0-2" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">cook the apple ingredients on the stovetop on medium heat for about 12 minutes and stir often. add 3 tbsp coconut cream at the end and cook another minute or two. let the mixture cool at least 10 minutes.</div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-23093-step-0-3" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">for the dough, add about 1/4 cup of dough to parchment paper cups and then slightly wet your fingers so you can mold the dough. otherwise, it will be too sticky. after that, lightly press on the dough from the edges and form a wide hole in the center where the apples will go.</div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-23093-step-0-4" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">bake at 350 degrees for 20 minutes. after you pull them out, quickly, gently and safely use a tbsp measuring spoon to press down the center because it will rise in the baking process (try not to break any crust off the sides).</div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-23093-step-0-5" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">add the sautéed apples to the center, drizzle a little maple syrup on each cup, and bake another 10 minutes at 350 degrees.</div></li><li id="wprm-recipe-23093-step-0-6" class="wprm-recipe-instruction" style="list-style-type: decimal;"><div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text" style="margin-bottom: 10px;">store in an airtight container in the fridge and enjoy!</div></li></ol></div></div>
      
      <div id="recipe-video"></div>
      
      <div class="wprm-spacer" style="height: 40px;"></div>
      
    </div>
  </div>
</div></div></div></div><!-- .entry-content -->
	</div>
</article><!-- #post-10205 -->
